		346 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		OR = {
				49 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				356 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				343 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }

	}

		TUR = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = TUR
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = TUR
				}
				remove_claim_by = TUR
			}
		}
		49 = { add_core_of = TUR }
		356 = { add_core_of = TUR }
		343 = { add_core_of = TUR }
		355 = { add_core_of = TUR }
		345 = { add_core_of = TUR }
		346 = { add_core_of = TUR }

			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = NFA
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = NFA
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = NFA} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TUR
			}
		}
		TUR = {

				state = 626
				state = 627
				state = 628
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				PHI = { exists = yes }
			}
			PHI = { is_subject_of = NFA }
		}
		327 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		623 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		624 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		625 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		626 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		627 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		628 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
		OR = {
				327 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				623 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				624 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				625 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				626 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				627 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
				628 = { NOT = { is_core_of = NFA } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		PHI = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = PHI
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = PHI
				}
				remove_claim_by = PHI
			}
		}
		327 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		623 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		624 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		625 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		626 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		627 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		628 = { add_core_of = PHI }
		release = PHI
		PHI = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = NFA
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = NFA
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = NFA} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PHI
			}
		}
		PHI = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = NFA_DGL_PHI_OCC

				name = "Administration Militaire Française"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDNFA/DeGaulle_Admin.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			NFA = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PHI
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 75
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "Administration Militaire Française"
				long_name = "Administration Militaire Française"
			}
		}
	}
